# [VS Code] Fix Stale TypeScript Diagnostics After Git Branch Switch

**Repository:** microsoft/vscode  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** big_code_feature
**Task Type:** Feature Implementation - Large Codebase

**Reference:** [Trevor's Big Code Research](../../../docs/TREVOR_RESEARCH_DEC2025.md#1-vs-code-stale-diagnostics-after-git-branch-switch)

## Description

Users are seeing stale TypeScript diagnostics in the Problems panel after switching Git branches. Files that no longer have errors still show the old errors until the user manually opens each file and makes an edit. It seems like the diagnostics pipeline only refreshes on in-editor changes and misses file-on-disk changes from Git operations.

## Task

This task requires implementing code changes to fix stale diagnostics.

### Required Implementation

Check the full diagnostics flow from a text change through the extension host to the Problems view, identify where file system changes should trigger diagnostic updates, and propose where we'd need to add listeners to fix this.

### Implementation Steps

1. **Understand the diagnostics pipeline**:
   - Find the main diagnostics collection and how it stores errors per file
   - Locate the extension host communication for sending diagnostics to the client
   - Find the Problems view panel and how it subscribes to diagnostics
   - Look for existing file change listeners (e.g., `deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile`, `onWillChange`)

2. **Identify where diagnostics are currently refreshed**:
   - Find the text change event handlers that trigger re-diagnostics
   - Understand how the diagnostics pipeline reacts to document changes
   - Look for any existing file system watchers or listeners

3. **Add file system change triggers**:
   - Add listener for file changes on disk (e.g., from `git checkout`)
   - Trigger diagnostics refresh for changed files
   - Clear stale diagnostics for files that no longer exist
   - Re-run TypeScript/language server analysis for affected files

4. **Test the fix**:
   - Switch branches that change TypeScript errors
   - Verify stale diagnostics are cleared
   - Verify new errors are shown after branch switch
   - No duplicate diagnostics appear

5. **Verify no regressions**:
   - All tests pass: `npm test`
   - No performance regression from additional file watchers
   - Diagnostics still work for in-editor changes

## Success Criteria

[x] Stale diagnostics are cleared when files change on disk  
[x] New diagnostics appear after Git branch switch  
[x] Diagnostics refresh without requiring manual file edits  
[x] Problems panel reflects current state of files  
[x] All tests pass: `npm test`  
[x] No performance regression  
[x] Code follows VS Code conventions and patterns  

## Testing

```bash
npm test
```

    15→
    16→function diagnosticsEquals(a: vscode.Diagnostic, b: vscode.Diagnostic): boolean {
    17→	if (a === b) {
    18→		return true;
    19→	}
    20→
    21→	return a.code === b.code
    22→		&& a.message === b.message
    23→		&& a.severity === b.severity
    24→		&& a.source === b.source
    25→		&& a.range.isEqual(b.range)
    26→		&& arrays.equals(a.relatedInformation || arrays.empty, b.relatedInformation || arrays.empty, (a, b) => {
    27→			return a.message === b.message
    28→				&& a.location.range.isEqual(b.location.range)
    29→				&& a.location.uri.fsPath === b.location.uri.fsPath;
    30→		})
    31→		&& arrays.equals(a.tags || arrays.empty, b.tags || arrays.empty);
    32→}

     1→#!/usr/bin/env bash
     2→set -e
     3→
     4→if [[ "$OSTYPE" == "darwin"* ]]; then
     5→	realpath() { [[ $1 = /* ]] && echo "$1" || echo "$PWD/${1#./}"; }
     6→	ROOT=$(dirname $(dirname $(realpath "$0")))
     7→else
     8→	ROOT=$(dirname $(dirname $(readlink -f $0)))
     9→	# --disable-dev-shm-usage: when run on docker containers where size of /dev/shm
    10→	# partition < 64MB which causes OOM failure for chromium compositor that uses the partition for shared memory
    11→	LINUX_EXTRA_ARGS="--disable-dev-shm-usage"
    12→fi
    13→
    14→cd $ROOT
    15→
    16→if [[ "$OSTYPE" == "darwin"* ]]; then
    17→	NAME=`node -p "require('./product.json').nameLong"`
    18→	CODE="./.build/electron/$NAME.app/Contents/MacOS/Electron"

	// Setup file system watcher to detect disk changes and refresh diagnostics
	// This fixes the issue where stale diagnostics appear after Git branch switches
	private setupDiskChangeWatcher(): void {
		// Create a file system watcher for TypeScript/JavaScript files
		const filePattern = new vscode.RelativePattern(
			vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] || vscode.workspace.workspaceFile || '/',
			'**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}'
		);

		const watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(filePattern, false, false, false);
		
		// When files are modified on disk, refresh diagnostics for open files
		const handleFileChange = (uri: vscode.Uri) => {
			// Only handle files that are currently tracked by buffer sync
			if (!this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(uri)) {
				return;
			}

			// Clear the stale diagnostics for this file
			this.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(uri);

			// Request new diagnostics to be computed
			if (this.bufferSyncSupport.ensureHasBuffer(uri)) {
				this.bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri]);
			}
		};

		this._register(watcher.onDidChange(handleFileChange));
		this._register(watcher);
	}

+	// Setup file system watcher to detect disk changes and refresh diagnostics
+	// This fixes the issue where stale diagnostics appear after Git branch switches
+	private setupDiskChangeWatcher(): void {
+		// Create a file system watcher for TypeScript/JavaScript files
+		const filePattern = new vscode.RelativePattern(
+			vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] || vscode.workspace.workspaceFile || '/',
+			'**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}'
+		);
+
+		const watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(filePattern, false, false, false);
+		
+		// When files are modified on disk, refresh diagnostics for open files
+		const handleFileChange = (uri: vscode.Uri) => {
+			// Only handle files that are currently tracked by buffer sync
+			if (!this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(uri)) {
+				return;
+			}
+
+			// Clear the stale diagnostics for this file
+			this.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(uri);
+
+			// Request new diagnostics to be computed
+			if (this.bufferSyncSupport.ensureHasBuffer(uri)) {
+				this.bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri]);
+			}
+		};

# Fix for Stale TypeScript Diagnostics After Git Branch Switch

## Problem
Users see stale TypeScript diagnostics in the Problems panel after switching Git branches. Files that no longer have errors still show the old errors until the user manually opens and edits each file.

##Root Cause
The diagnostics pipeline only refreshes when:
1. A text document is edited in the editor
2. A document is opened/closed
3. The editor visibility changes

It does NOT refresh when files change on disk (from Git operations or other external changes).

## Solution
Add a file system watcher that detects when TypeScript/JavaScript files change on disk and triggers a diagnostics refresh for those files.

## Changes Required

### File: extensions/typescript-language-features/src/typescriptServiceClient.ts

#### Change 1: Line 199 - Call setupDiskChangeWatcher on ready
**Old:**
```typescript
		this.onReady(() => { this.bufferSyncSupport.listen(); });
```

**New:**
```typescript
		this.onReady(() => { this.bufferSyncSupport.listen(); this.setupDiskChangeWatcher(); });
```

#### Change 2: Add new method before `configurePlugin` (around line 1241)
**Add this new method:**
```typescript
	// Setup file system watcher to detect disk changes and refresh diagnostics
	// This fixes the issue where stale diagnostics appear after Git branch switches
	private setupDiskChangeWatcher(): void {
		// Create a file system watcher for TypeScript/JavaScript files
		const filePattern = new vscode.RelativePattern(
			vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] || vscode.workspace.workspaceFile || '/',
			'**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}'
		);

		const watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(filePattern, false, false, false);
		
		// When files are modified on disk, refresh diagnostics for open files

I've encountered a file system permission issue that's preventing me from directly modifying the VS Code source code. The repository files are owned by root and I don't have write permissions. However, I've completed the analysis and created the complete solution.

Let me summarize what needs to be done to fix the stale diagnostics issue:

## Problem Identified
The TypeScript diagnostics pipeline in VS Code only refreshes when text is edited in the editor, but it does NOT refresh when files change on disk (e.g., from Git branch switches). This causes stale diagnostics to remain in the Problems panel.

## Solution: Add a Disk Change Watcher

The fix requires adding a file system watcher in `extensions/typescript-language-features/src/typescriptServiceClient.ts` that:

1. **Detects file changes on disk** for all TypeScript/JavaScript files
2. **Clears stale diagnostics** for changed files using `diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile()`
3. **Requests fresh analysis** via `bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri])`

### Complete Modified File

I've prepared the complete modified file at: `/tmp/typescriptServiceClient_modified.ts`

The two specific changes are:

**Line 199** - Add setupDiskChangeWatcher call:
```typescript
this.onReady(() => { this.bufferSyncSupport.listen(); this.setupDiskChangeWatcher(); });
```

The editor visibility changes\n\nIt does NOT refresh when files change on disk (from Git operations or other external changes).\n\n## Solution\nAdd a file system watcher that detects when TypeScript/JavaScript files change on disk and triggers a diagnostics refresh for those files.\n\n## Changes Required\n\n### File: extensions/typescript-language-features/src/typescriptServiceClient.ts\n\n#### Change 1: Line 199 - Call setupDiskChangeWatcher on ready\n**Old:**\n```typescript\n\t\tthis.onReady(() => { this.bufferSyncSupport.listen(); });\n```\n\n**New:**\n```typescript\n\t\tthis.onReady(() => { this.bufferSyncSupport.listen(); this.setupDiskChangeWatcher(); });\n```\n\n#### Change 2: Add new method before `configurePlugin` (around line 1241)\n**Add this new method:**\n```typescript\n\t// Setup file system watcher to detect disk changes and refresh diagnostics\n\t// This fixes the issue where stale diagnostics appear after Git branch switches\n\tprivate setupDiskChangeWatcher(): void {\n\t\t// Create a file system watcher for TypeScript/JavaScript files\n\t\tconst filePattern = new vscode.RelativePattern(\n\t\t\tvscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] || vscode.workspace.workspaceFile || '/',\n\t\t\t'**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}'\n\t\t);\n\n\t\tconst watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(filePattern, false, false, false);\n\t\t\n\t\t// When files are modified on disk, refresh diagnostics for open files\n\t\tconst handleFileChange = (uri: vscode.Uri) => {\n\t\t\t// Only handle files that are currently tracked by buffer sync\n\t\t\tif (!this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(uri)) {\n\t\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Clear the stale diagnostics for this file\n\t\t\tthis.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(uri);\n\n\t\t\t// Request new diagnostics to be computed\n\t\t\tif (this.bufferSyncSupport.ensureHasBuffer(uri)) {\n\t\t\t\tthis.bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri]);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t};\n\n\t\tthis._register(watcher.onDidChange(handleFileChange));\n\t\tthis._register(watcher);\n\t}\n```\n\n## How It Works\n\n1. **File System Watcher**: Creates a watcher for `**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}` files in the workspace\n2. **Change Detection**: When a file changes on disk (detected via `onDidChange`), the handler is called\n3. **Buffer Check**: Only processes files that are currently in bufferSyncSupport (open files)\n4. **Diagnostics Refresh**: \n   - Clears stale diagnostics for the file\n   - Ensures the file is in the buffer\n   - Requests new diagnostics via `bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri])`\n\n## Benefits\n\n- Stale diagnostics are cleared when files change on disk\n- New diagnostics appear after Git branch switches\n- No manual file edits required\n- Minimal performance impact (only triggers for files in bufferSyncSupport)\n- Uses existing DiagnosticsManager and bufferSyncSupport APIs\n\n## Testing\n\nAfter applying these changes:\n\n1. Create a TypeScript file with an error\n2. Switch Git branches where that error no longer exists\n3. Verify the diagnostic disappears from the Problems panel immediately\n4. 21. $ cat > /tmp/fix_diagnostics.ts << 'EOF'
	// Setup file system watcher to detect disk changes and refresh diagnostics
	// This fixes the issue where stale diagnostics appear after Git branch switches
	private setupDiskChangeWatcher(): void {
		// Create a file system watcher for TypeScript/JavaScript files
		const filePattern = new vscode.RelativePattern(
			vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] || vscode.workspace.workspaceFile || '/',
			'**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}'
		);

		const watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(filePattern, false, false, false);
		
		// When files are modified on disk, refresh diagnostics for open files
		const handleFileChange = (uri: vscode.Uri) => {
			// Only handle files that are currently tracked by buffer sync
			if (!this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(uri)) {
				return;
			}

			// Clear the stale diagnostics for this file
			this.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(uri);

			// Request new diagnostics to be computed
			if (this.bufferSyncSupport.ensureHasBuffer(uri)) {
				this.bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri]);
			}
		};

		this._register(watcher.onDidChange(handleFileChange));
		this._register(watcher);
	}
EOF
cat /tmp/fix_diagnostics.ts

47. $ cat > /tmp/DIAGNOSTICS_FIX_SUMMARY.md << 'EOF'
# Fix for Stale TypeScript Diagnostics After Git Branch Switch

## Problem
Users see stale TypeScript diagnostics in the Problems panel after switching Git branches. Files that no longer have errors still show the old errors until the user manually opens and edits each file.

##Root Cause
The diagnostics pipeline only refreshes when:
1. A text document is edited in the editor
2. A document is opened/closed
3. The editor visibility changes

It does NOT refresh when files change on disk (from Git operations or other external changes).

## Solution
Add a file system watcher that detects when TypeScript/JavaScript files change on disk and triggers a diagnostics refresh for those files.

## Changes Required

### File: extensions/typescript-language-features/src/typescriptServiceClient.ts

#### Change 1: Line 199 - Call setupDiskChangeWatcher on ready
**Old:**
```typescript
		this.onReady(() => { this.bufferSyncSupport.listen(); });
```

**New:**
```typescript
		this.onReady(() => { this.bufferSyncSupport.listen(); this.setupDiskChangeWatcher(); });
```

#### Change 2: Add new method before `configurePlugin` (around line 1241)
**Add this new method:**
```typescript
	// Setup file system watcher to detect disk changes and refresh diagnostics
	// This fixes the issue where stale diagnostics appear after Git branch switches
	private setupDiskChangeWatcher(): void {
		// Create a file system watcher for TypeScript/JavaScript files
		const filePattern = new vscode.RelativePattern(
			vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] || vscode.workspace.workspaceFile || '/',
			'**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}'
		);

		const watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(filePattern, false, false, false);
		
		// When files are modified on disk, refresh diagnostics for open files
		const handleFileChange = (uri: vscode.Uri) => {
			// Only handle files that are currently tracked by buffer sync
			if (!this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(uri)) {
				return;
			}

			// Clear the stale diagnostics for this file
			this.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(uri);

			// Request new diagnostics to be computed
			if (this.bufferSyncSupport.ensureHasBuffer(uri)) {
				this.bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri]);
			}
		};

		this._register(watcher.onDidChange(handleFileChange));
		this._register(watcher);
	}
```

## How It Works

1. **File System Watcher**: Creates a watcher for `**/*.{ts,tsx,js,jsx}` files in the workspace
2. **Change Detection**: When a file changes on disk (detected via `onDidChange`), the handler is called
3. **Buffer Check**: Only processes files that are currently in bufferSyncSupport (open files)
4. **Diagnostics Refresh**: 
   - Clears stale diagnostics for the file
   - Ensures the file is in the buffer
   - Requests new diagnostics via `bufferSyncSupport.getErr([uri])`

## Benefits

- Stale diagnostics are cleared when files change on disk
- New diagnostics appear after Git branch switches
- No manual file edits required
- Minimal performance impact (only triggers for files in bufferSyncSupport)
- Uses existing DiagnosticsManager and bufferSyncSupport APIs

## Testing

After applying these changes:

1. Create a TypeScript file with an error
2. Switch Git branches where that error no longer exists
3. Verify the diagnostic disappears from the Problems panel immediately
4. Verify new errors appear if the branch has different errors
5. Run: `npm run test-extension` to verify no regressions

EOF

cat /tmp/DIAGNOSTICS_FIX_SUMMARY.md
